layout: "post"
title: "The circle"
date: "2018-05-01"
agda: true
toc: true
categories: type-theory
---

In this entry, we want to show some equivalences
between the circle and other higher inductive types.

{% comment %}

{: . equation }

  $$\sum\,{\mathbb{S}^1}\,(\mathsf{rec}_{\mathbb{S}^1}\, \mathcal{U}\,  2\,
  (\mathsf{ua}(\mathsf{rec}_{2}2 1_{2} 0_{2}))) \simeq \mathbb{S}^1.$$

I gave a talk giving one solution using the flattening lemma:

- [**Direct link PDF**](https://github.com/jonaprieto/flattenlem/files/2045561/Jonathan-Prieto-Cubides-The-Flattening-Lemma.pdf)

{% endcomment %}

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="616" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="620" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="628" class="Option">--without-K</a> <a id="640" class="Symbol">#-}</a>
<a id="644" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="649" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="656" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}" class="Module">2018-07-06-mini-hott</a>
<a id="677" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="684" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}" class="Module">_</a> <a id="686" class="Keyword">where</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

##  S¹ type

The circle is the higher inductive type with one point
and one no trivial path called path as we show in the following
picture.

![path](/assets/ipe-images/circle.png)
*Figure 1. The circle type `S¹`.*

  <a id="1867" class="Keyword">postulate</a>

## Equivalences

### Lemma 1

{: .equation }

  $$ \mathsf{S}^{1} \simeq \mathsf{pS}. $$

**Proof**.

Let us define the outgoing functions:

<a id="4484" class="Keyword">private</a>

In the following, we will need the following term:
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="4772" class="Comment">-- Def.</a>

The proof of the homotopy $$ f' ∘ g' \sim \mathsf{id}$$.

### Lemma 2

- Action on paths of pairs

### Lemma 3

{: .equation}
  $$
    \Sigma~S^{1}~P~\simeq~pS
  $$

  where $$P (\mathsf{base}) :≡ \mathsf{Bool}$$ and $$\mathsf{ap~P~loop~=~ua~(neg)}$$.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="12094" class="Comment">-- Def.</a>
<a id="neg"></a><a id="12102" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#12102" class="Function">neg</a> <a id="12106" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12108" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3672" class="Datatype">Bool</a> <a id="12113" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12115" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3672" class="Datatype">Bool</a>
<a id="12120" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#12102" class="Function">neg</a> <a id="12124" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3693" class="InductiveConstructor">true</a>  <a id="12130" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12132" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3708" class="InductiveConstructor">false</a>
